                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Sunday
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_mkZhg3NDgY/VA0EGTvIsPI/AAAAAAAAfrc/OgUTkKk5Dfk/s1600/cats401.gif" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="646176238650463330" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="2187012259505710997" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="2187012259505710997">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     35 Crazy Cats That Will Have You Die Laughing.
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2187012259505710997" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_mkZhg3NDgY/VA0EGTvIsPI/AAAAAAAAfrc/OgUTkKk5Dfk/s1600/cats401.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" height="243" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_mkZhg3NDgY/VA0EGTvIsPI/AAAAAAAAfrc/OgUTkKk5Dfk/s1600/cats401.gif" width="320"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Cats Are Crazy
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        A cats eyesight is both better and worse than humans. It is better because cats can see in much dimmer light and they have a wider peripheral view. Its worse because they dont see color as well as humans do. Scientists believe grass appears red to cats.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Spanish-Jewish folklore recounts that Adams first wife, Lilith, became a black vampire cat, sucking the blood from sleeping babies. This may be the root of the superstition that a cat will smother a sleeping baby or suck out the childs breath.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Perhaps the most famous comic cat is the Cheshire Cat in Lewis Carrolls Alice in Wonderland. With the ability to disappear, this mysterious character embodies the magic and sorcery historically associated with cats.f
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        In the original Italian version of Cinderella, the benevolent fairy godmother figure was a cat.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Two Siamese cats discovered microphones hidden by Russian spies in Hollands embassy in Moscow In Hollands embassy in Moscow, Russia, the staff noticed that the two Siamese cats kept meowing and clawing at the walls of the building. Their owners finally investigated, thinking they would find mice. Instead, they discovered microphones hidden by Russian spies. The cats heard the microphones when they turned on.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        The little tufts of hair in a cats ear that help keep out dirt direct sounds into the ear, and insulate the ears are called ear furnishings.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        The ability of a cat to find its way home is called psi-traveling. Experts think cats either use the angle of the sunlight to find their way or that cats have magnetized cells in their brains that act as compasses.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Isaac Newton invented the cat flap. Newton was experimenting in a pitch-black room. Spithead, one of his cats, kept opening the door and wrecking his experiment. The cat flap kept both Newton and Spithead happy.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div>
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="buzz_superlist_item buzz_superlist_item_grid_row buzz_superlist_item_wide " id="superlist_3414621_3582498" rel:buzz_num="1" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; clear: both; color: #111111; font-size: 12px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 20px 0px; position: relative;">
                       <h2 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-size: 26px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                         <span class="buzz_superlist_number_inline" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; display: inline; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          1.
                         </span>
                         When you jump into the air, you fall back to the ground. Because gravity.
                        </span>
                       </h2>
                       <div class="grid_row one grid_height_m" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; float: left; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; width: 625px;">
                        <div class="grid_cell cell_1" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; float: left; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         <div class="grid_cell_image_wrapper" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; float: left; line-height: 0; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px; position: relative;">
                          <div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; height: 309px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px; width: 625px;">
                           <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                            <b>
                             <img height="351" rel:bf_image_src="http://s3-ec.buzzfed.com/static/2014-08/12/6/enhanced/webdr07/anigif_enhanced-29175-1407839401-1.gif" src="http://s3-ec.buzzfed.com/static/2014-08/12/6/enhanced/webdr07/anigif_enhanced-29175-1407839401-1.gif" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; left: 0px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; top: -11px; width: 624px;" width="624"/>
                            </b>
                           </span>
                          </div>
                          <a class="animatedgifs button-rubbable bf_dom" href="https://www.blogger.com/null" rel:bf_bucket="animatedgifs" rel:gt_act="rub/list-item:1" rel:gt_label="/static/2014-08/13/5/enhanced/webdr07/grid-cell-31536-1407922469-11.jpg" style="background: url(http://s3-ak.buzzfed.com/static/images/public/posts/rubbable-finger.png); border: 0px; color: #0077ee; cursor: pointer; display: block; height: 27px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: absolute; right: 2px; top: 3px; visibility: visible; width: 27px;">

                         <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                          <b>
                           Isaac Newton first described the force of gravity. But he couldnt really explain

                       <h2 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-size: 26px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                         <span class="buzz_superlist_number_inline" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; display: inline; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          2.
                         </span>
                         Matter bends space, and thats how gravity is transmitted.
                        </span>
                       </h2>

                       <h2 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-size: 26px; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">

                         <span class="buzz_superlist_number_inline" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; display: inline; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          4.

                        </span>

                     window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();

              }
            }
          });

      });
